Prerequisites
Make sure you have the following installed on your system:

Node.js (version 14 or higher)

npm (Node Package Manager, comes with Node.js)

You can check if Node.js and npm are installed by running these commands in your terminal:

bash
Copy
node -v
npm -v
If not installed, download and install Node.js from nodejs.org.

2. Download the Project
If you haven't already, download or clone the project files to your local machine.

3. Install Dependencies
Navigate to the project directory (where package.json is located) and run:

bash
Copy
npm install
This will install all the required dependencies listed in package.json.

4. Start the Server
To start the backend server, run:

bash
Copy
npm start
or, if you want to run it in development mode with automatic restarts (using nodemon), use:

bash
Copy
npm run dev
You should see a message in the terminal like:

Copy
Library Management System running at http://localhost:3000
5. Access the Application
Open your web browser and go to:

Copy
http://localhost:3000
You should see the Library Management System interface.

6. Add, Edit, and Manage Books
Use the form to add new books.

Search and sort books using the controls.

Edit or delete books using the action buttons in the table.

Export the data as a CSV file using the "Export Data" button.

7. Stop the Server
To stop the server, press Ctrl + C in the terminal where the server is running.

8. (Optional) Debugging
If you encounter any errors, check the terminal for logs.

Ensure the books.csv file exists in the project directory. If not, the server will create it automatically.

If you make changes to the code, restart the server (Ctrl + C and then npm start again).

9. (Optional) Run in Production
If you want to deploy the application to a production environment:

Install a process manager like pm2:

bash
Copy
npm install -g pm2
Start the application with pm2:

bash
Copy
pm2 start index.js
Monitor the application:

bash
Copy
pm2 logs

class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre"><span><span>http:</span><span><span class="hljs-comment">//localhost:3000  </span></span><span>
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="1314" data-end="1375">You should now see the Library Management System interface.</p>
<hr data-start="1377" data-end="1380">
<h2 data-start="1382" data-end="1417">6. Add, Edit, and Manage Books</h2>
<ul data-start="1419" data-end="1645">
<li data-start="1419" data-end="1457">Use the form to <strong data-start="1437" data-end="1454">add new books</strong>.</li>
<li data-start="1458" data-end="1507"><strong data-start="1460" data-end="1479">Search and sort</strong> books using the controls.</li>
<li data-start="1508" data-end="1579"><strong data-start="1510" data-end="1518">Edit</strong> or <strong data-start="1522" data-end="1532">delete</strong> books using the action buttons in the table.</li>
<li data-start="1580" data-end="1645"><strong data-start="1582" data-end="1597">Export data</strong> as a CSV file using the "Export Data" button.</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="1647" data-end="1650">
<h2 data-start="1652" data-end="1675">7. Stop the Server</h2>
<p data-start="1676" data-end="1759">To stop the server, press <code data-start="1702" data-end="1712">Ctrl + C</code> in the terminal where the server is running.</p>
<hr data-start="1761" data-end="1764">
<h2 data-start="1766" data-end="1794">8. (Optional) Debugging</h2>
<p data-start="1796" data-end="1826">If you encounter any errors:</p>
<ul data-start="1828" data-end="2095">
<li data-start="1828" data-end="1872">Check the <strong data-start="1840" data-end="1857">terminal logs</strong> for details.</li>
<li data-start="1873" data-end="1993">Ensure the <strong data-start="1886" data-end="1899">books.csv</strong> file exists in the project directory. (The server will create it automatically if missing.)</li>
<li data-start="1994" data-end="2095">If you make changes to the code, restart the server:

<ol data-start="68" data-end="496">
<li data-start="68" data-end="136">
<p data-start="71" data-end="136"><strong data-start="71" data-end="100">Click on the file preview</strong> (where the content is displayed).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="137" data-end="216">
<p data-start="140" data-end="216"><strong data-start="140" data-end="155">Right-click</strong> anywhere inside the content area and select <strong data-start="200" data-end="213">"Save As"</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="217" data-end="331">
<p data-start="220" data-end="331"><strong data-start="220" data-end="240">Save the file as</strong> <code data-start="241" data-end="252">README.md</code> — make sure the file extension is <code data-start="287" data-end="292" data-is-only-node="">.md</code> for GitHub to recognize it properly.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="332" data-end="496">
<p data-start="335" data-end="409"><strong data-start="335" data-end="371">Upload it to your project folder</strong> or push it to your repository with:</p>

max(3rem, 24vh);"><div class="_main_5jn6z_1 z-10 markdown prose contain-inline-size dark:prose-invert focus:outline-none bg-transparent ProseMirror ProseMirror-focused" contenteditable="true" style="width: 580px;" translate="no"><h1><span>Library Management System - Setup Guide</span></h1><h2><span>1. Prerequisites</span></h2><p><span>Make sure you have the following installed on your system:</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><strong><span>Node.js</span></strong><span> (version 14 or higher)</span></p></li><li><p><strong><span>npm</span></strong><span> (Node Package Manager, comes with Node.js)</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>Check if Node.js and npm are installed</span></h3><p><span>Run these commands in your terminal:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ16 ͼrp" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" data-language="shell" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ19">node</span> <span class="ͼ19">-v</span>  </div><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ19">npm</span> <span class="ͼ19">-v</span>  </div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5px; height: 19px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><p><span>If not installed, download and install Node.js from </span><a href="https://nodejs.org/" disabled="false"><span>nodejs.org</span></a><span>.</span></p><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>2. Download the Project</span></h2><p><span>If you haven't already, download or clone the project files to your local machine:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ16 ͼrq" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" data-language="shell" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ19">git</span> clone &lt;repository-url&gt;</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5px; height: 19px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>3. Install Dependencies</span></h2><p><span>Navigate to the project directory (where </span><code><span>package.json</span></code><span> is located) and run:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ16 ͼrr" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" data-language="shell" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ19">npm</span> install  </div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5px; height: 19px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><p><span>This will install all the required dependencies listed in </span><code><span>package.json</span></code><span>.</span></p><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>4. Start the Server</span></h2><p><span>To start the backend server, run:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ16 ͼrs" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" data-language="shell" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ19">npm</span> <span class="ͼ19">start</span>  </div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5px; height: 19px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><p><span>Or, for development mode with automatic restarts (using </span><strong><span>nodemon</span></strong><span>):</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ16 ͼrt" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" data-language="shell" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ19">npm</span> run dev  </div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5px; height: 19px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><p><span>You should see a message in the terminal like:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ16 ͼru" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line">Library Management System running at http://localhost:3000  </div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5px; height: 19px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>5. Access the Application</span></h2><p><span>Open your web browser and visit:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ16 ͼrv" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line">http://localhost:3000  </div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5px; height: 19px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><p><span>You should now see the Library Management System interface.</span></p><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>6. Add, Edit, and Manage Books</span></h2><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Use the form to </span><strong><span>add new books</span></strong><span>.</span></p></li><li><p><strong><span>Search and sort</span></strong><span> books using the controls.</span></p></li><li><p><strong><span>Edit</span></strong><span> or </span><strong><span>delete</span></strong><span> books using the action buttons in the table.</span></p></li><li><p><strong><span>Export data</span></strong><span> as a CSV file using the "Export Data" button.</span></p></li></ul><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>7. Stop the Server</span></h2><p><span>To stop the server, press </span><code><span>Ctrl + C</span></code><span> in the terminal where the server is running.</span></p><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>8. (Optional) Debugging</span></h2><p><span>If you encounter any errors:</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Check the </span><strong><span>terminal logs</span></strong><span> for details.</span></p></li><li><p><span>Ensure the </span><strong><span>books.csv</span></strong><span> file exists in the project directory. (The server will create it automatically if missing.)</span></p></li><li><p><span>If you make changes to the code, restart the server:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ16 ͼrw" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" data-language="shell" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line">Ctrl <span class="ͼ1e">+</span> C  </div><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ19">npm</span> <span class="ͼ19">start</span>  </div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5px; height: 19px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div></li></ul><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>9. class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div></li><li><p><span>Start the application with </span><strong><span>pm2</span></strong><span>:</span></p><div
